<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afkomst.html>afkomst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">origin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.

</p>
<ol><li>originating
<ul><li><b>2003</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Ibn_Battuta" class="extiw" title="w:nl:Ibn Battuta">Dutch Wikipedia on Ibn Battuta</a>
<dl><dd>Ibn Battuta <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> Berberse <a href = vnd.unilang:reiziger.html>reiziger</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:auteur.html>auteur</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:afkomstig.html>afkomstig</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tanger.html>Tanger</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huidige.html>huidige</a> Marokko.
<dl><dd>Ibn Battuta <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a Berber traveller and author, originating from <a href = vnd.unilang:tanger.html>Tanger</a> in present-day Morocco.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

</p>

***afleggen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afleggen.html>afleggen</a> (5280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:afleggen.html>afleggen</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aveleggen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*abalagjaną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leggen.html>leggen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afleggen.html>afleggen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cover (e.g. a distance)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Zonnevliegtuig <b><a href = vnd.unilang:legt.html>legt</a></b> recordafstand <b><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Solar-powered aircraft <b><a href = vnd.unilang:covers.html>covers</a></b> a record distance.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i> as the object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to perish, to <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i> as the object</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be defeated</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to prepare a deceased person for the funeral</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afnemen.html>afnemen</a> (4640)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:afnemen.html>afnemen</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">avenemen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">avaneman</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*abanemaną</i>; equivalent to  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nemen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to decrease

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afnemer.html>afnemer</a> (39859)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afnemen.html>afnemen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afnemer.html>afnemer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afnemers.html>afnemers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">organisation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">customer</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">client</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">buyer</span> (of goods or services)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">profession</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">buyer</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">purchaser</span>, one who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> busy with <span class="Latn" lang="en">procurement</span> professionally</li></ol>

***afschieten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afschieten.html>afschieten</a> (11826)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:afschieten.html>afschieten</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schieten.html>schieten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afschieten.html>afschieten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shoot dead, to kill by firing at someone or something</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cull</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to descend quickly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to separate or to divide with an object such as a screen or a wall</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shoot, to fire <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to launch a projectile, to use a range weapon</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to separate with a barrier</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Southern</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pay, to pay up</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to plunder, to rob
<ul><li><b>1838</b>, Adriaan <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>Hoop</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:junior.html>Junior</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Renegaat. <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> berymd <a href = vnd.unilang:verhaal.html>verhaal</a></i>, Elix amp; co., 80-81.
<dl><dd><i>On ne se souvient plus <a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:promesses.html>promesses</a>, quand <a href = vnd.unilang:les.html>les</a> périls <a href = vnd.unilang:sont.html>sont</a> passés</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zegt.html>zegt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> fransche <a href = vnd.unilang:spreekwoord.html>spreekwoord</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:motto.html>motto</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Algerijnen <a href = vnd.unilang:immer.html>immer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schreven.html>schreven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> teboekstellen <a href = vnd.unilang:hunner.html>hunner</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdragen.html>verdragen</a>; want by <a href = vnd.unilang:iedere.html>iedere</a> verademing, <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> eene ontfangene tuchtiging, <b>schuimden</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> Korsaren den <a href = vnd.unilang:oceaan.html>Oceaan</a> roofgieriger <b><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ooit.html>ooit</a>.
<dl><dd><i>One no longer follows through on promises, when the threats have passed</i>, says the French proverb: it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the <i><a href = vnd.unilang:motto.html>motto</a></i> that the Algerians always <a href = vnd.unilang:wrote.html>wrote</a> on the codifications of their treaties; for during every respite, after a received punitive expedition, those Corsairs <b>plundered</b> the ocean more rapaciously than ever.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2010</b>, Jan Cremer, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hunnen.html>Hunnen</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bezig.html>Bezige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>Bij</a>, 754.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b>schuimden</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:straten.html>straten</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:kwamen.html>kwamen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vooral.html>vooral</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:donker.html>donker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schuilplaatsen.html>schuilplaatsen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tevoorschijn.html>tevoorschijn</a>.
<dl><dd>They <b>plundered</b> the streets, and <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> out of their hiding <a href = vnd.unilang:places.html>places</a> mostly under the cover of darkness.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2014</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:kate.html>Kate</a> Williams, <i> Joséphine. <a href = vnd.unilang:verlangen.html>Verlangen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ambitie.html>ambitie</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:napoleon.html>Napoleon</a></i>, Prometheus.
<dl><dd>Roversbendes <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zakkenrollers.html>zakkenrollers</a> <b>schuimden</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:straten.html>straten</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moorden.html>moorden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:orde.html>orde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afschuw.html>afschuw</a> (17256)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">afschuwen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:shoo.html>shoo</a> off, <a href = vnd.unilang:shoo.html>shoo</a> away</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Abscheu</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">avsky</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">afsky</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afschuw.html>afschuw</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>revulsion, abhorrence, repugnance, horror, abomination <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">strong aversion</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sluiten.html>sluiten</a></i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afsluiten.html>afsluiten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to close off, seal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> waterkering <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sluit.html>sluit</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> IJsselmeer <b><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Waddenzee.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The embankment <b>closes off</b> the IJssel Lake from the Wadden Sea.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to conclude, to end, to terminate</li></ol>
